ูููู:ูจ [1mRight high and mighty prince, and my right noble, and after one leivest (earthly) lord [0m

I recommend me unto your grace with all my heart. And as you desire the welfare of the king our sovereign lord, and of his realms 
of England and France, your own weal (health), with all yours haste you hither; For, by my troth, if you tarry long, we shall put 
this land in jeopardy (adventure) with a field; such a brother you have here; God make him a good man. For your wisdom well 
knoweth that the profit of France standeth in the welfare of England etc. The blessed Trinity keeps you. Written in a great haste 
at London, on Allhalloweneven. 

the 3l [1mst of October, 1425 

By your servant, to my lives end 

Henry Winchester
